Late Yelp Post (1/23/2016):
One of my favorite go-to places for a quick bite to eat in the morning. I love their chorizo burrito, and ham&cheese croissant sandwiches! They make fresh orange juice but it's a bit pricey. My boyfriend and I always come here for a well done breakfast bagel and burrito. He gets the breakfast bagel and I get the chorizo (with egg and cheese) burrito. They are both delicious! I cannot get enough of their freshly squeezed orange juice machine, although I feel like the machine wastes more oranges than needed. Their hot chocolate is also exceptional!<//review>

Update Review: 10-18-2018

I love the spicy chicken tenders and today for some reason It was super good. The food was very good and most of all, all the staff was awesome great customer service all round.

Harry Irvine

Update Review: 02-24-2018

I had the spicy chicken with biscuits and a small drink. Food was very fresh and good, as the service it was very slow and the cashier did not know that my combo came with a side order. I think the staff needs to be trained here.

Harry Irvine

If you like to eat Chicken, then this is the spot for it, very hot and spicy and let me say a few things here:

They Cook the chicken per your order that is why its HOT and SPICY so good.

Very small place but worth the wait so if your in a rush I recommend that you call your order in.

Parking...no problem plenty of parking

Customer service: at the time I was there it was perfect the staff was nice and helpful.

Overall, just some great Chicken, Thank you Popeyes</text>
